"<s1>Human:RDC中页面:抽屉-同步价格 组件名称:SelectHook 业务名称: "需求工厂",F下拉框 组件,元属性/元数据怎么编写？</s1>
<s1>Assisnt:元数据内容如下:
```
{"type":"SelectHook","isForm":true,"property":{"enabled":false,"componentTypeName":"","mode":"single","showAdd":false,"dataSource":{"url":"/md/plant/findpagebycondition","type":"api","serverName":"mdorg","method":"post","bodyExpression":"resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: '386b4f94e98d400e94f17f7c0bdde470', data: '@@formValues' } }).then(params => {\r\n    // debugger\r\n    callback({\r\n        materialCode: params.materialCode || \"\",\r\n        purchasingOrgCode: params.purchasingOrgCode || \"\",\r\n        variables: {\r\n            page: { page: 1, pageSize: 20 }\r\n        }\r\n    })\r\n})"},"sceneStyle":"","displayMode":false,"filed":"plantCode","subscribes":[{"event":"795771c1379c4c1fa1351f07045e27b4.onChange","pubs":[{"event":"","eventPayloadExpression":"// pubsub.publish('@@message.error', '$${BID.message.please.select.bidding.details.first}')\r\n      pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {\r\n         id: '2cc2e97ef8b1405998609c868636b7a1',\r\n         data: [\r\n            {\r\n               name: 'plantCode', value: null,\r\n            }, {\r\n               name: 'plantName', value: null,\r\n            }\r\n         ],\r\n      })\r\n ```
```
在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || 
// 当前的物料
const currMats = eventPayload.$AllParams.customs.data
console.log("currMats=", currMats)

let { plantName, plantCode, materialName, contractNo, contractRowNo,
    purchasingGroupCode, purchasingGroupName,    
    materialCode, effectiveDate, expirationDate,
    pricingUnitCode, pricingUnitName, orderUnitCode, orderUnitName, scalingId, scalingMatDtlId,extendPlantCodeList, extendPlantNameList } = currMats

const { vendorCode, vendorName } = currMats
//价格有效期
const effectDate = { startTime: effectiveDate, endTime: expirationDate }

//采购组织编码
const purchasingOrgCode = currMats.scaling.purchasingOrgCode


//展示用的字段
const _showMaterialName = `${materialCode} - ${materialName}`

//先用物料编码查一遍物料主数据
let dataSource = {
    type: 'api',
    method: 'post',
    serverName: 'auction',
    url: `/aucauctionscaling/getmaterialbycode`,
    body: JSON.stringify({
        materialCode,
        plantCode,
    })
};
resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {

    if (response.success) {

        let mats = response.data
        //交货不足限度 过量交货限度 计划天数 默认从主数据带出
        const { baseUnitName, baseUnitCode,
            numerator,  // 订单单位<=>基本单位 分子
            denominator,      // 订单单位<=>基本单位 分母
            pricingUnitMolecule,// 定价单位 <=> 基本单位 分子
            orderUnitCode: defaultOrderUnitCode,// 定价单位 <=> 基本单位 分子
            orderUnitName: defaultOrderUnitName//订单单位空的话，默认取主数据的
        } = mats

        let { overDeliveryLimit, shortDeliveryLimit, planDays } = mats.materialPlants || {}


        //从物料主数据带出的 先除100
        //overDeliveryLimit && (overDeliveryLimit = parseFloat((overDeliveryLimit / 100).toPrecision(12)))
        //shortDeliveryLimit && (shortDeliveryLimit = parseFloat((shortDeliveryLimit / 100).toPrecision(12)))

        orderUnitCode = orderUnitCode || defaultOrderUnitCode
        orderUnitName = orderUnitName || defaultOrderUnitName

        let elementaryUnit = orderUnitCode == baseUnitCode ? 1 : currMats.elementaryUnit || denominator
        //定价单位 <=>基本单位分母
        let baseUnitDenominator = pricingUnitCode == baseUnitCode ? 1 : currMats.baseUnitDenominator || denominator

        overDeliveryLimit = currMats.overDeliveryLimit || overDeliveryLimit
        shortDeliveryLimit = currMats.shortDeliveryLimit || shortDeliveryLimit

        pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
            id: "386b4f94e98d400e94f17f7c0bdde470",
            data: {
                vendorCode,
                vendorName,
                materialName,
                materialCode,
                _showMaterialName,
                overDeliveryLimit: overDeliveryLimit ? Math.round(overDeliveryLimit) : null,
                shortDeliveryLimit: shortDeliveryLimit ? Math.round(shortDeliveryLimit) : null,
                planDays: currMats.planDays || planDays,
                elementaryUnitName: baseUnitName,
                elementaryUnitCode: baseUnitCode,
                orderElementaryUnit: numerator || 1,
                elementaryUnit: elementaryUnit,
                pricingUnitMolecule: currMats.pricingUnitMolecule || pricingUnitMolecule || 1,
                pricingUnitCode,
                pricingUnitName,
                baseUnitDenominator,
                orderUnitCode,
                orderUnitName,
                orderUnitName,
                scalingId,
                scalingMatDtlId,
                effectDate,
                purchasingGroupCode,
                purchasingGroupName,
                purchasingOrgCode,               
                plantName,
                plantCode,
                contractNo,
                extendPlantCodeList, 
                extendPlantNameList
            }
        });
        pubsub.publish('7da28208974f4941976feeb2ef585849.loadData', { clearValue: false })
        
        //扩展工厂
        pubsub.publish('5d20452444ca4cf68b31d81ed2e26693.loadData', { clearValue: false })

        //如果采购组织原本就存在 则不可修改
        if (purchasingGroupCode) {
            pubsub.publish('618f09987e294f78ba888de5f6b9ab0c.enabled', false)
        }


        //如果有合同行号 合同不能选择和修改
        // if (contractRowNo) {
        //     pubsub.publish('bee2b27fe87f43e389842aa4b1dd892c.enabled', false)
        // }
        // pubsub.publish('1c60bf8f22214ff18b69f36817764e93.visible', !contractRowNo)

    } else {
        pubsub.publish('@@message', response.message)
    }


});



```
</s1>"
"<s1>Human:RDC中页面:抽屉-同步价格 组件名称:SelectHook 业务名称: "扩展工厂",F下拉框 组件,元属性/元数据怎么编写？</s1>
<s1>Assisnt:元数据内容如下:

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || 
// 当前的物料
const currMats = eventPayload.$AllParams.customs.data
console.log("currMats=", currMats)

let { plantName, plantCode, materialName, contractNo, contractRowNo,
    purchasingGroupCode, purchasingGroupName,    
    materialCode, effectiveDate, expirationDate,
    pricingUnitCode, pricingUnitName, orderUnitCode, orderUnitName, scalingId, scalingMatDtlId,extendPlantCodeList, extendPlantNameList } = currMats

const { vendorCode, vendorName } = currMats
//价格有效期
const effectDate = { startTime: effectiveDate, endTime: expirationDate }

//采购组织编码
const purchasingOrgCode = currMats.scaling.purchasingOrgCode


//展示用的字段
const _showMaterialName = `${materialCode} - ${materialName}`

//先用物料编码查一遍物料主数据
let dataSource = {
    type: 'api',
    method: 'post',
    serverName: 'auction',
    url: `/aucauctionscaling/getmaterialbycode`,
    body: JSON.stringify({
        materialCode,
        plantCode,
    })
};
resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {

    if (response.success) {

        let mats = response.data
        //交货不足限度 过量交货限度 计划天数 默认从主数据带出
        const { baseUnitName, baseUnitCode,
            numerator,  // 订单单位<=>基本单位 分子
            denominator,      // 订单单位<=>基本单位 分母
            pricingUnitMolecule,// 定价单位 <=> 基本单位 分子
            orderUnitCode: defaultOrderUnitCode,// 定价单位 <=> 基本单位 分子
            orderUnitName: defaultOrderUnitName//订单单位空的话，默认取主数据的
        } = mats

        let { overDeliveryLimit, shortDeliveryLimit, planDays } = mats.materialPlants || {}


        //从物料主数据带出的 先除100
        //overDeliveryLimit && (overDeliveryLimit = parseFloat((overDeliveryLimit / 100).toPrecision(12)))
        //shortDeliveryLimit && (shortDeliveryLimit = parseFloat((shortDeliveryLimit / 100).toPrecision(12)))

        orderUnitCode = orderUnitCode || defaultOrderUnitCode
        orderUnitName = orderUnitName || defaultOrderUnitName

        let elementaryUnit = orderUnitCode == baseUnitCode ? 1 : currMats.elementaryUnit || denominator
        //定价单位 <=>基本单位分母
        let baseUnitDenominator = pricingUnitCode == baseUnitCode ? 1 : currMats.baseUnitDenominator || denominator

        overDeliveryLimit = currMats.overDeliveryLimit || overDeliveryLimit
        shortDeliveryLimit = currMats.shortDeliveryLimit || shortDeliveryLimit

        pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
            id: "386b4f94e98d400e94f17f7c0bdde470",
            data: {
                vendorCode,
                vendorName,
                materialName,
                materialCode,
                _showMaterialName,
                overDeliveryLimit: overDeliveryLimit ? Math.round(overDeliveryLimit) : null,
                shortDeliveryLimit: shortDeliveryLimit ? Math.round(shortDeliveryLimit) : null,
                planDays: currMats.planDays || planDays,
                elementaryUnitName: baseUnitName,
                elementaryUnitCode: baseUnitCode,
                orderElementaryUnit: numerator || 1,
                elementaryUnit: elementaryUnit,
                pricingUnitMolecule: currMats.pricingUnitMolecule || pricingUnitMolecule || 1,
                pricingUnitCode,
                pricingUnitName,
                baseUnitDenominator,
                orderUnitCode,
                orderUnitName,
                orderUnitName,
                scalingId,
                scalingMatDtlId,
                effectDate,
                purchasingGroupCode,
                purchasingGroupName,
                purchasingOrgCode,               
                plantName,
                plantCode,
                contractNo,
                extendPlantCodeList, 
                extendPlantNameList
            }
        });
        pubsub.publish('7da28208974f4941976feeb2ef585849.loadData', { clearValue: false })
        
        //扩展工厂
        pubsub.publish('5d20452444ca4cf68b31d81ed2e26693.loadData', { clearValue: false })

        //如果采购组织原本就存在 则不可修改
        if (purchasingGroupCode) {
            pubsub.publish('618f09987e294f78ba888de5f6b9ab0c.enabled', false)
        }


        //如果有合同行号 合同不能选择和修改
        // if (contractRowNo) {
        //     pubsub.publish('bee2b27fe87f43e389842aa4b1dd892c.enabled', false)
        // }
        // pubsub.publish('1c60bf8f22214ff18b69f36817764e93.visible', !contractRowNo)

    } else {
        pubsub.publish('@@message', response.message)
    }


});



```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || 
resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: "fdf27db1f28c449a9cec36e6e94e988c", data: "@@formValues" } }).then(function (result) {
    const { priceEffectiveTo, plantCode, materialCode, purchasingOrgCode, purchasingGroupCode,
        purchaseCategory, filter } = result;
    var newFilter = filter;
    const currentHistorySort = result.currentHistorySort || 0
    if (plantCode && plantCode.length > 0) {
        newFilter += " and plantCode in ('" + plantCode[0];

        if (plantCode.length > 1) {
            for (var i = 1; i < plantCode.length; i++) {
                newFilter += "','" + plantCode[i];
            }
        }
        newFilter += "')";
    }
    if (priceEffectiveTo != undefined && priceEffectiveTo != '') {
        let start = getSubtractDate(priceEffectiveTo, " 00:00:00");
        let end = getSubtractDate(0, " 23:59:59");
        if (priceEffectiveTo != 0) {
            newFilter += " and effectiveDate ge '" + start + "' ";

        }
        newFilter += " and effectiveDate le '" + end + "' ";
    }
    let dataSource = {
        type: 'api',
        method: 'post',
        url: '/smdmaterialmasterpriceapply/list',
        body: JSON.stringify({ filter: newFilter, pageSize: 500, sorted: 'effectiveDate asc' }),
        serverName: 'sourcing'
    };
    resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {
        let data = response.data || []
        pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
            id: "fdf27db1f28c449a9cec36e6e94e988c",
            name: "historyPriceData",
            value: data
        });
        if (currentHistorySort == 0) {
            pubsub.publish("0eca0bfc5aed4e54806b10e86cd9e184.setData", data)
        } else {
            pubsub.publish("fdf27db1f28c449a9cec36e6e94e988c.setHistoryPriceChart")
        }

    });
});

function getSubtractDate(subtractDays, endWith) {
    var date = new Date();
    date = date.setDate(date.getDate() - subtractDays)
    date = new Date(date);
    var sept = "-";
    var year = date.getFullYear();
    var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
    var strDate = date.getDate();
    if (month >= 1 && month <= 9) {
        month = "0" + month;
    }
    if (strDate >= 0 && strDate <= 9) {
        strDate = "0" + strDate;
    }
    var str = year + sept + month + sept + strDate;
    return str + endWith;
}

```
</s1>"

```
    sourceId: gid,
    purchasingOrgCode,

                recordUserCode: User.userCode,

        source: 'sourcingType_002',
        sourceNo: bidNo,
        sourceId: gid,
    }],
    // _souceObj: eventPayload.$AllParams.state.data,

    bidId,
    bidNo
}

    id: "3455e101e35c4e129ad5100115be6eae",

})
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
. || const params = eventPayload.$AllParams.state;
if (params.data && params.data.type) {
    //来自那个页面 detail 详情页
    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', { id: 'e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e', name: 'type', value: params.data.type })
}
if (params.mode == 'modify') {
    pubsub.publish("e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e.getMainInfo", params.data.bidId)
    pubsub.publish("21c3ffdf3e274c74882dee1b43308f52.visible", true)//状态标签
    pubsub.publish("15e12aa88df9451a9df275e7a26b55c2.visible", true)//保存按钮
    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
        id: 'e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e',
        name: 'mode',
        value: 'modify'
    })
} else if (params.mode == 'add') {
   initByAdd()
} else if (eventPayload.$AllParams.search.bidId) {
    pubsub.publish("e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e.getMainInfo", eventPayload.$AllParams.search.bidId)
    pubsub.publish("4157c0e0eb9549ebb388f5cbb8c4e92f.visible", true)//暂存按钮
    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
        id: 'e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e',
        name: 'mode',
        value: 'copy'
    })
} else if(eventPayload.$AllParams.search.draftId){
    let formData = {
        draftId: eventPayload.$AllParams.search.draftId
    }
    // 从草稿箱调过来的暂存数据
    pubsub.publish("4157c0e0eb9549ebb388f5cbb8c4e92f.visible", true)//暂存
    pubsub.publish("e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e.getDraft", formData.draftId);
}else{
    initByAdd()
}

// //初始化业务员数据
// pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
//     id: 'e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e',
//     name: 'salesman',
//     value: JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("userInfo")).userName
// })


function initByAdd(){
     pubsub.publish('e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e-title.setLabel', '$${label.newBid}')
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish("4157c0e0eb9549ebb388f5cbb8c4e92f.visible", true)//暂存按钮
        pubsub.publish('cfe0855628374ecf8add8a0bea329e75.visible', false);//评标模板
        pubsub.publish('0dce12ee139b4cf9945e06c8f7f40b5a.visible', false);//评标专家
        pubsub.publish('0a2d7042d58f4504b706e36d7ec0b65a.visible', true) //资质证书
    }, 200)

    const { userId, userName, mobile } = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('userInfo')) || {}
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e",
        data: [
            { name: 'salesmanName', value: userName },
            { name: 'salesmanUserId', value: userId },
            { name: 'scoreMethod', value: 'unEval' },
            { name: 'bidType', value: 'InviteTenders' },
            { name: 'bidContactTelNo', value: mobile },
            { name: "openSort", value: "openSort_001" },//同时
            { name: "tendSort", value: "tendSort_001" },//同时
            { name: 'invoiceType', value: 'incremen' },
            { name: "bidEvalType", value: "bidEvalType_003" }, //不评标
            { name: "isPrequalify", value: "1" },// 需要预审
            { name: 'quoteType', value: 'bidQuoteType_001' },//捆绑报价
            { name: "bidOpenType", value: "bidOpenType_001" },//有开标确认
            { name: "numberLadder", value: "numberLadder_002" }, //供应商定义
            { name: "bidWay", value: "bidWay_001" }//线上招标
        ]
    });
    //招标小组表格id
    pubsub.publish('56e7a3716edd452b8537b48ad0c60b9d.initGroup')
    //阶段信息初始化
    pubsub.publish('0101e57cbfbf41d886ed2b8b4448cb16.initByOrder')
}
```

```
            { name: 'scoreMethod', value: 'unEval' },
            { name: 'bidType', value: 'InviteTenders' },
            { name: 'bidContactTelNo', value: mobile },
            { name: "openSort", value: "openSort_001" },//同时
            { name: "tendSort", value: "tendSort_001" },//同时
            { name: 'invoiceType', value: 'incremen' },
            { name: "bidEvalType", value: "bidEvalType_003" }, //不评标
            { name: "isPrequalify", value: "1" },// 需要预审
            { name: 'quoteType', value: 'bidQuoteType_001' },//捆绑报价
            { name: "bidOpenType", value: "bidOpenType_001" },//有开标确认
            { name: "numberLadder", value: "numberLadder_002" }, //供应商定义
            { name: "bidWay", value: "bidWay_001" }//线上招标
        ]
    });
    //招标小组表格id
    pubsub.publish('56e7a3716edd452b8537b48ad0c60b9d.initGroup')
    //阶段信息初始化
    pubsub.publish('0101e57cbfbf41d886ed2b8b4448cb16.initByOrder')
}
```

```
 ||     // Type you code ...
    resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: "e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e", data: "@@formValues" } }).then(function (result) {
        if (result.numberLadder !== result.tempNumberLadderName &&
            result.numberLadder !== "numberLadder_001" && result.matDtlList &&
            result.matDtlList.length > 0) {
            //采购方切换为供应商方  有物料已设置数量阶梯
            let matDtlList = result.matDtlList || [];
            let mats = matDtlList.filter((item) => {
                if (item.hasNumberLadder == "$${label.yes}") return item
            }) || []



            if (!mats.length) {
                controlLadderCol(result.numberLadder)
                return
            }
            pubsub.publish('e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e.openConfirmM', {
                title: '$${message.prompt}',
                content: "$${Common.tip.numberLadderChanged}",
                onOk: () => {
                    //清掉数量阶梯
                    matDtlList.forEach((item) => {
                        item.hasNumberLadder = "$${label.no}";
                        item.matNumLadderDtlList = [];
                    })
                    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                        id: "e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e",
                        name: "matDtlList",
                        value: matDtlList
                    })
                    controlLadderCol(result.numberLadder)
                },
                onCancel: () => {
                    controlLadderCol('numberLadder_001')
                    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", { id: 'e693de1e9acf466ba76d31642a82768e', name: 'numberLadder', value: 'numberLadder_001', })
                }
            })
        } else {
            controlLadderCol(result.numberLadder)
        }


        function controlLadderCol(code) {
            console.log(code)
            //供应商定义的话 隐藏数量阶梯列
            const show = code == 'numberLadder_001'

            pubsub.publish(`4fc3393aaaa8497eaf569e2b991ce8e0.setColShowAndHide`, {
                colIds: ['b6b148c89f5d4a7ca6ffccf3b5970b2e'],
                visible: show
            })

        }
    });
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || 
let formData = Object.assign(
    {},
    eventPayload.$AllParams.state.data,
    {
        type: eventPayload.$AllParams.search.type
    }
)

// if (formData.type == "add") {//新建
//     pubsub.publish('0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602-title.setLabel', "$${CTC.field.newContractTemplate}")
//     pubsub.publish("0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602.sourceField")
// } else 
if (formData.type == "copy") {//复制
    pubsub.publish('0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602-title.setLabel', "$${CTC.field.newContractTemplate}")
    pubsub.publish("0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602.copyGetMainInfo",{
        templateId:formData.templateId,
        templateNo:formData.templateNo,
    })
} else if (formData.type == "edit") {//编辑
    pubsub.publish('0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602-title.setLabel',"$${CTC.field.editContractTemplate} "+ formData.templateNo)
    pubsub.publish('6c627f200fc3458ca2aaba1317b124f4.visible',true); //状态
    pubsub.publish('664a05e2ef2a45c0949c7e269b2286c3.visible',false); //新建-提交
    pubsub.publish('1a66832f4f7d4e15ac26f15c50317331.visible',false); //暂存
    pubsub.publish('9ed7b0381e834001800503ce3c7e36e7.visible',true); //编辑-提交
    pubsub.publish('2235d13c8f374a22853c68d501c5a96d.visible',true); //编辑-保存
    pubsub.publish("0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602.editGetMainInfo",{
        templateId:formData.templateId,
        templateNo:formData.templateNo,
    })
} else {//草稿箱
    let formData = {
        draftId: eventPayload.$AllParams.search.draftId
    }
    pubsub.publish('0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602-title.setLabel', "$${CTC.field.newContractTemplate}")
    if(formData.draftId){
        pubsub.publish("0a4b23cf176c4f24a16e81429a8b7602.getDraft", formData.draftId);
    }
}
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
@@form.init || const { unitConvert, NP } = window.MAIN_COMMON_UTILS
let formData = eventPayload.$AllParams.state
let searchData = eventPayload.$AllParams.search
pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.getcontrolpointvalue', {})
if (formData.type == 'add') {
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
        data: [{
            name: "type",
            value: formData.type
        }]
    });
    pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newPrefabricatedInvoice}')
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('b1f55ab345ce4594b26e16e3401701ec.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
    })

} else if (formData.type == 'edit') {
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
        data: [{
            name: "type",
            value: formData.type
        }]
    });
    pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.editPreInvoice}' + ' ' + formData.data.preInvoiceCode)
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('6f760d14760d4bb5b1860c7994f12481.visible', true)/**保存按钮 */
        pubsub.publish('ea9179cadeb44929b9bb770ea2dace8f.visible', true)/**状态标签 */
    })
    // pubsub.publish('4345e5fccaab4fbbbf865b9a9dc542f6.enabled', false)/**对账类别 */
    // pubsub.publish('f5b30d1f0c4846a580dbe900c3c72e43.enabled', false)/**采购组织 */
    // pubsub.publish('9106087c9a12496c8641a03b4d9ca0e0.enabled', false)/**公司 */
    // pubsub.publish('e2d67b445ed546e2a46790dfdc273896.enabled', false)/**货币 */
    // pubsub.publish('4a39aadf396540ca99518cc5b7949208.enabled', false)/**供应商 */
    /**先初始化主单 */
    pubsub.publish("246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.getMainInfo", formData.data);

    setTimeout(() => {
        if (formData.init) {
            delete formData.init
        }
        pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
            id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
            name: "init",
            value: null
        });
    }, 5000)
} else if (searchData.type == 'copy' || searchData.type == 'copy1') {/**对账==》开票 */
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
        data: [{
            name: "type",
            value: searchData.type
        }]
    });
    pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newPrefabricatedInvoice}')
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('b1f55ab345ce4594b26e16e3401701ec.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
    })


    // var receiptBill
    // if (searchData.type == 'copy') {
    //     receiptBill = JSON.parse(searchData.receiptBill)
    // } else if (searchData.type == 'copy1') {
    //     receiptBill = [JSON.parse(searchData.receiptBill)]
    // }
    // receiptBill.forEach(item => {
    //     item.taxRateValue = item.taxRate
    //     item.taxRateUpValue = item.taxRate * 100
    //     item.receiptBillCode = item.receiptBill.receiptBillCode
    //     item.receiveBillNo = item.receivebillNo
    //     if (item.acceptReturnFlag == 101) {
    //         item.returnFlag = '收货'
    //     } else if (item.acceptReturnFlag == 102) {
    //         item.returnFlag = '退货'
    //     }
    // })
    // var mainInit = {
    //     type: searchData.type,
    //     billType: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.billType,
    //     companyCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyCode,
    //     companyName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyName,

    //     vendorName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorName,
    //     currencyCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencyCode,
    //     currencyName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencyName,
    //     currencySymbol: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencySymbol,
    //     purchasingOrgCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgCode,
    //     purchasingOrgName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgName,
    //     // list: receiptBill
    // }
    // setTimeout(() => {
    //     pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
    //         id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
    //         data: mainInit
    //     });
    //     setTimeout(() => {
    //         pubsub.publish('9106087c9a12496c8641a03b4d9ca0e0.loadData', { clearValue: false })/**公司 */

    //         pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
    //             id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
    //             name: "list",
    //             value: receiptBill
    //         });
    //         setTimeout(() => {
    //             if (searchData.init) {
    //                 delete searchData.init
    //             }
    //         }, 4000)
    //     }, 1000)
    // }, 200)
    // if (receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyCode && receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorCode) {//调用管控点
    //     pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.getcontrolpointvalue', receiptBill[0].receiptBill)
    // }

    //2023.4 修改，对账【新建预制发票】需要的信息进入发票页面后再通过接口获取

    console.log("searchData", searchData)

    let dataSource = {
        type: 'api',
        method: 'post',
        serverName: 'finance',
        url: '/fireceiptbill/invoiceablepagepur',
        bodyExpression: `callback({pageSize: -1, filter:" srcMaterialCertificate in (${searchData.srcMaterialCertificate})"})`
    };
    resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {
        var receiptBill;
        receiptBill = response.data;
        receiptBill.forEach(item => {
            item.taxRateValue = item.taxRate
            item.taxRateUpValue = item.taxRate * 100
            item.receiptBillCode = item.receiptBill.receiptBillCode
            item.receiveBillNo = item.receivebillNo
            if (item.acceptReturnFlag == 101) {
                item.returnFlag = '收货'
            } else if (item.acceptReturnFlag == 102) {
                item.returnFlag = '退货'
            }

            //明细临时字段
            item.pricingQty = item.fixPriceQty//定价单位数量
            item.fixPriceQty = item.canInvQty//可开票数量（定价单位数量）            
            item.orderQty = item.orderSettlementQty//订单单位数量
            debugger
            //根据结算数量（定价数量/订单数量比例）算出订单单位可结算数量
            let { pricingQty, orderQty, fixPriceQty } = item
            if (pricingQty && orderQty && fixPriceQty) {
                let orderSettlementQty = NP.divide(NP.times(fixPriceQty, orderQty), pricingQty)
                let convertRes = unitConvert(item.unitCode, orderSettlementQty) //与计量单位的小数位数一致
                item.orderSettlementQty = convertRes.convertQuantity//订单单位可结算数量
            }
            item.initQty = item.canInvQty//可开票数量（定价单位数量）
            item.maxQty = item.canInvQty//结算数量上限 
            item.settlementAmountTax = item.canInvSettlementAmountTax//可开票含税金额
            item.settlementAmountNoTax = item.canInvSettlementAmountNoTax//可开票未税金额
            item.settlementTax = NP.minus(item.settlementAmountTax, item.settlementAmountNoTax)//结算税额
        })
        var mainInit = {
            type: searchData.type,
            billType: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.billType,
            companyCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyCode,
            companyName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyName,
            vendorErpCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorErpCode,
            vendorCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorCode,
            vendorName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorName,
            currencyCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencyCode,
            currencyName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencyName,
            currencySymbol: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.currencySymbol,
            purchasingOrgCode: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgCode,
            purchasingOrgName: receiptBill[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgName,
            init: '1'
            // list: receiptBill
        }
        setTimeout(() => {
            pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
                id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
                data: mainInit
            });
            setTimeout(() => {
                pubsub.publish('9106087c9a12496c8641a03b4d9ca0e0.loadData', { clearValue: false })/**公司 */
                pubsub.publish('4a39aadf396540ca99518cc5b7949208.loadData', { clearValue: false })/**供应商 */

                pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                    id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
                    name: "list",
                    value: receiptBill
                });
                //触发费用列表加载
                pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.feeInfo', { type: 'change' })
                setTimeout(() => {
                    if (searchData.init) {
                        delete searchData.init
                    }
                    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                        id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
                        name: "init",
                        value: null
                    });
                }, 4000)
            }, 1000)
        }, 200)
        if (receiptBill[0].receiptBill.companyCode && receiptBill[0].receiptBill.vendorCode) {//调用管控点
            pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.getcontrolpointvalue', receiptBill[0].receiptBill)
        }


    });


} else if (searchData.type == 'fee') {/**费用-开票 */
    pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newPrefabricatedInvoice}')
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('b1f55ab345ce4594b26e16e3401701ec.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
    })
    var feeBillData = JSON.parse(searchData.feeBillData)
    feeBillData.forEach(item => {
        item.taxRateUpValue = item.taxRateValue * 100
        item.receiptBillId = item.receiptBill.receiptBillId
    })
    var mainInit = {
        type: searchData.type,
        billType: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.billType,
        companyCode: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.companyCode,
        companyName: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.companyName,
        vendorErpCode: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.vendorErpCode,
        vendorCode: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.vendorCode,
        vendorName: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.vendorName,
        currencyCode: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.currencyCode,
        currencyName: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.currencyName,
        currencySymbol: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.currencySymbol,
        purchasingOrgCode: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgCode,
        purchasingOrgName: feeBillData[0].receiptBill.purchasingOrgName,
    }
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
            id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
            data: mainInit
        });
        setTimeout(() => {
            pubsub.publish('9106087c9a12496c8641a03b4d9ca0e0.loadData', { clearValue: false })/**公司 */
            pubsub.publish('4a39aadf396540ca99518cc5b7949208.loadData', { clearValue: false })/**供应商 */

            pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                id: "246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea",
                name: "feeList",
                value: feeBillData
            });
        }, 1000)
    }, 200)
} else {
    pubsub.publish('246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newPrefabricatedInvoice}')
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('b1f55ab345ce4594b26e16e3401701ec.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
    })
    let draftData = {
        draftId: eventPayload.$AllParams.search.draftId,
        type: eventPayload.$AllParams.state.type
    }
    pubsub.publish("246657916abe44738999f614592b54ea.getDraft", draftData.draftId);
}
```

<s1>Assisnt:元数据内容如下:
```
{"property":{"enabled":true,"componentTypeName":"","mode":"single","showAdd":false,"dataSource":{"method":"post","serverName":"mdgeneric","bodyExpression":"callback({\r\n    groupCode: \"PaymentBillSourceType\"\r\n})","type":"api","url":"/md/datadict/getall"},"sceneStyle":"","displayMode":false,"filed":"paymentBillSourceType","subscribes":[{"pubs":[{"event":"","eventPayloadExpression":"pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {\r\n    id: 'b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3',\r\n    name: 'paymentBillSourceType',\r\n    value: 'BS01'\r\n})"}],"event":"3ec8d68055814b9bb8e76cb0e8faa595.initValue"}],"valueField":"itemCode","showFiled":"","multiCols":false,"remoteSearch":false,"multiColsConfig":[],"showRequiredStar":true,"onLoadData":true,"labelAlign":"","displayAuto":"","isDescription":false,"visible":true,"placeholder":"$${label.please.choose}","multiPagination":false,"multipleColor":"","valueAlign":"","label":"$${FI.label.paymentApplicationSource}","defaultOption":false,"tagStyle":"{}","displayField":"itemName","wordColor":"","pagination":{"pageNoField":"variables.page.page","pageSizeField":"variables.page.pageSize","filterField":"variables.filter","totalField":"pager.totalRecords","disabled":false,"hideOnSinglePage":false,"simple":false,"small":true},"id":"3ec8d68055814b9bb8e76cb0e8faa595","description":"付款申请来源","propType":"SelectHook","isMapRequest":false,"wrapperSpan":24,"labelSpan":24,"showRefresh":true,"singleValidate":["required"]},"type":"SelectHook","isForm":true}
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
@@form.init || let formData = eventPayload.$AllParams.state.data || eventPayload.$AllParams.search
pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
    id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
    data: [
        { name: "type", value: formData.type }
    ]
});

if (formData.type == 'add') {
    pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newApplication}')
    // pubsub.publish('da9946dbf0af4477a8efe4225a61ad96.visible', false)/**预付卡片 */
    // pubsub.publish('5e7c4e384d864c048a80d1437198ca67.visible', false)/**索赔卡片 */
    pubsub.publish('005cf972218f4f9abb33989311b8b4e0.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
} else if (formData.type == 'edit') {
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
        data: [
            { name: "init", value: true }
        ]
    });
    pubsub.publish('da9946dbf0af4477a8efe4225a61ad96.visible', true)/**预付卡片 */
    pubsub.publish('5e7c4e384d864c048a80d1437198ca67.visible', true)/**索赔卡片 */
    pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.editPaymentRequest}' + ' ' + formData.paymentBillCode)
    /**先初始化主单 */
    pubsub.publish("b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3.getMainInfo", formData);
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
        name: "ven",
        value: "1"
    });
} else if (formData.type == 'copy') {
    pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newApplication}')
    pubsub.publish('005cf972218f4f9abb33989311b8b4e0.visible', true)/**暂存按钮 */
    pubsub.publish('da9946dbf0af4477a8efe4225a61ad96.visible', true)/**预付卡片 */
    pubsub.publish('5e7c4e384d864c048a80d1437198ca67.visible', true)/**索赔卡片 */
    var invoice = JSON.parse(formData.invoice)
    // pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
    //     id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
    //     name: "purchasingOrgCode",
    //     value: invoice[0].purchasingOrgCode
    // });
    // pubsub.publish('e5465ee81f47460baa928a3dbedd229d.loadData')/**公司 */
    // pubsub.publish('2160f01b303e489d9e8dfcfa9c8fb3e6.loadData')/**供应商 */
    invoice.forEach(item => {
        item.applyPayAmount = Number(item.unPaidAmount)
        item.dataStatus = '1'
    })
    //设置当前日期
    var date = new Date();
    var seperator1 = "-";
    var year = date.getFullYear();
    var month = date.getMonth() + 1;
    var strDate = date.getDate();
    if (month >= 1 && month <= 9) {
        month = "0" + month;
    }
    if (strDate >= 0 && strDate <= 9) {
        strDate = "0" + strDate;
    }
    var currentdate = year + seperator1 + month + seperator1 + strDate;
    var mainInfo = {
        purchasingOrgCode: invoice[0].purchasingOrgCode,
        purchasingOrgName: invoice[0].purchasingOrgName,
        companyCode: invoice[0].companyCode,
        companyName: invoice[0].companyName,
        vendorCode: invoice[0].vendorCode,
        vendorErpCode: invoice[0].vendorErpCode,
        vendorName: invoice[0].vendorName,
        currencyCode: invoice[0].currencyCode,
        currencyName: invoice[0].currencyName,
        currencySymbol: invoice[0].currencySymbol,
        paymentBillSourceType: 'BS01',
        applyPayTime: currentdate,
        type: 'copy',
        init: true
    }
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
            id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
            data: mainInfo
        });
        setTimeout(() => {
            pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3.findvendorbankdtlall')/**查询供应商银行 */
            pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3.claimListLoading')/**加载索赔明细 */
            pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3.prePayListLoad')/**加载预付明细 */
            pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                id: "b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3",
                name: "invoiceRequestList",/**发票明细 */
                value: invoice
            });
            // 防止初始化默认只有一个值赋值的时候触发值变化
            setTimeout(() => {
                pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                    id: 'b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3',
                    name: 'init',
                    value: false
                });

            }, 2000)
        }, 1000)
    }, 100)
} else {/**从草稿箱调过来的暂存数据 */
    pubsub.publish('b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3-title.setLabel', '$${FI.label.newApplication}')
    pubsub.publish("b847d533d7024f468f1e85f70804fda3.getDraft", formData.draftId);
}
```

"<s1>Human:RDC中页面:共用-采购订单/需求池-新增/编辑 组件名称:SelectHook 业务名称: "点收方式",F下拉框 组件,元属性/元数据怎么编写？</s1>
<s1>Assisnt:元数据内容如下:
```
{"property":{"enabled":false,"componentTypeName":"","mode":"single","showAdd":false,"dataSource":{"method":"post","serverName":"mdgeneric","bodyExpression":"callback({\n    groupCode: \"receiveType\"\n})","type":"api","url":"/md/datadict/getall"},"sceneStyle":"","displayMode":false,"filed":"receiveType","subscribes":[],"valueField":"itemCode","showFiled":"","multiCols":false,"remoteSearch":false,"multiColsConfig":[],"showRequiredStar":true,"onLoadData":true,"labelAlign":"","displayAuto":"","isDescription":false,"visible":true,"placeholder":"$${label.pleaseSelect}","multiPagination":false,"multipleColor":"","valueAlign":"","label":"$${label.countMethod}","defaultOption":false,"tagStyle":"{}","displayField":"itemName","wordColor":"","pagination":{"pageNoField":"variables.page.page","pageSizeField":"variables.page.pageSize","filterField":"variables.filter","totalField":"pager.totalRecords","disabled":false,"hideOnSinglePage":false,"simple":false,"small":true},"id":"54c2287669c24f66a744f942b12ff6ae","description":"点收方式","propType":"SelectHook","isMapRequest":false,"wrapperSpan":24,"labelSpan":24,"showRefresh":true,"singleValidate":["required"]},"type":"SelectHook","isForm":true,"colId":"2563fbe53f46428193d9b87d2252698d","id":"54c2287669c24f66a744f942b12ff6ae"}
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || //解决编辑初始化弹窗问题
const dataSource = {
    type: 'api',
    serverName: 'purchasing',
    method: 'get',
    url: '/pecpurchaseorder/get',
    bodyExpression: "callback(" + JSON.stringify({
        purchaseOrderNo: eventPayload.purchaseOrderNo
    }) + ",'')",
    isLoading:true
}
const detail = {
    type: 'api',
    serverName: 'purchasing',
    method: 'get',
    url: '/pecpurchaseorder/getdetail',
    bodyExpression: "callback(" + JSON.stringify({
        purchaseOrderNo: eventPayload.purchaseOrderNo
    }) + ",'')",
    isLoading:true
}
let formData
const init = () => {
    resolveDataSource({ dataSource }).then(async (res) => {
        console.log('res', res)
        if (res.success || res.code == '0000') {
            const data = res.data,
                result = await resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: '338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c', data: '@@formValues' } });
                formData = Object.assign(
                    data,
                    {
                        type: 'modify',
                        pageId: eventPayload.pageId,
                        init: true,//初始化标识，获取数据渲染的时候先置为true，明细返回后延时三秒改为false，避免初始化赋值触发值变化中的事件
                        isReturn: result.isReturn,
                        h_details: result.purchaseOrderDetails,
                    }
                );
            pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
                id: "338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c",
                data: formData
            });
            console.log("getInfo =====",formData)
            if(String(formData.isReturn)=='1') {
                pubsub.publish('23e8c60f0c964b14870b963ddde68d7e.visible',false)  //不显示采购申请
                pubsub.publish('96a8f6dc59bf49219cbd89d1fbb4eee2.visible',false)  //不显示临时物料
            }else {
                pubsub.publish('23e8c60f0c964b14870b963ddde68d7e.visible',true)  //不显示采购申请
                pubsub.publish('338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c.getcontrolpoint')
            }
            
            pubsub.publish('f92f2309ad2d4d4f879968f12856bf30.getCompanyPlant',formData.companyCode)
            pubsub.publish('cf59c5a5a1164ef3a57a3d3e158086d8.getPurchasingOrgPlant',formData.purchasingOrgCode)
            if(eventPayload.pageId == '17588012fcaf4a439d35cf3637672569'){//采购订单
                pubsub.publish('17588012fcaf4a439d35cf3637672569-title.setLabel', "$${label.edit}$${label.purchaseOrder} " + eventPayload.purchaseOrderNo) 
            }else if(eventPayload.pageId == '7b1f32d9baaa4969b1f8e47ec4e6de18'){//需求池
                pubsub.publish('7b1f32d9baaa4969b1f8e47ec4e6de18-title.setLabel', "$${label.edit} " + eventPayload.purchaseOrderNo)
            }
            //公司带出的货币
            pubsub.publish('f92f2309ad2d4d4f879968f12856bf30.getStandCurrency', formData.companyCode)
        } else {
            pubsub.publish('@@message.error', res.message);
        }
    }).then(() => {
        //进入编辑页面时公司组件下拉框是默认不加载的，
        //所以需要重新加载公司下拉框(加载下拉框时回清空对应的数据，所以需要重新再进行赋值)
        pubsub.publish('f92f2309ad2d4d4f879968f12856bf30.loadData',{clearValue:false})

        //重新加载供应商下拉框
        pubsub.publish('5b923847f8b74aecbf8d70a28fea83df.loadData',{clearValue:false})
        resolveDataSource({ dataSource: detail }).then(res => {
            if (res.success || res.code == '0000') {

                let newData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(res.data))
                console.log( '获取明细数据')
                let purchaseCategory = newData[0]&&newData[0].hasOwnProperty('purchaseCategory')?newData[0].purchaseCategory:'';
                let isReturn = newData[0]&&newData[0].hasOwnProperty('isReturn')?newData[0].isReturn:'';

                pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
                    id:"338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c",
                    name:"purchaseCategory",
                    value:purchaseCategory
                });
                // 若所选择的[采购订单类型]设置为标准采购，并且费用化采购标识为“否”，
                // 并且是否退货为“否”并且点收方式为“送货点收”显示字段[源供应标识]，允许编辑,默认值为“否”,其余情况不显示
                if(purchaseCategory == '0' && formData.expenseFlag == 0 && isReturn == '0'&& formData.receiveType == 'R002') {
                    pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                        colIds: ['74b0921688664c73acaf3fad7bb7489f'],//源供应标识
                        visible: true
                    })
                }
                if(purchaseCategory == '0' && formData.expenseFlag == 1) {  
                    pubsub.publish('0eddd2b601224289b4b7408c310a5949.enabled',false);
                    pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                        colIds: ['4d24f13ac2c4415d8cdcf80c34f4a6ce'],
                        visible: true
                    })
                }else {
                    pubsub.publish('0eddd2b601224289b4b7408c310a5949.enabled',true);
                }
                if(purchaseCategory == '2') {
                    pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                        colIds: ['bc896055a6044084b3e754a8274c99e6'],
                        visible: false
                    })
                    pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColEnabled`, {
                        colIds: ['7a4a6b1be2284b18b434d482a6a8f2ce'],
                        visible: false
                    })
                }
                
                (newData||[]).forEach(item => {
                    const unitInfo = JSON.parse(item.unitConversionInfo)[0]
                    item = Object.assign(item, {
                        materialCode: item.materialCode ? item.materialCode : '-',
                        baseUnitCode: unitInfo.baseUnitCode,
                        baseUnitName: unitInfo.baseUnitName,
                        baseUnitDenominator: unitInfo.baseUnitDenominator,
                        pricingUnitMolecule: unitInfo.pricingUnitMolecule,
                        sourceVendorFlag:(item.sourceVendorFlag||item.sourceVendorFlag==0)?item.sourceVendorFlag.toString():'',
                        elementaryUnit: unitInfo.elementaryUnit,
                        pricingUnit: unitInfo.pricingUnit,
                        orderElementaryUnit: unitInfo.orderElementaryUnit,
                        orderPricingUnit: unitInfo.orderPricingUnit,
                        skuQty: unitInfo.skuQty,
                        shortDeliveryLimit: item.shortDeliveryLimit * 100,
                        overDeliveryLimit: item.overDeliveryLimit * 100,
                        //双单位转换信息
                        purchaseDualUnitConversions: [unitInfo],
                        taxRateUpValue: item.taxRateValue * 100,
                        basedOnReceiptFlag : item.basedOnReceiptFlag?item.basedOnReceiptFlag.toString():'',
                        isReturn : item.isReturn.toString()

                    })
                })
                    console.log('明细数据')
                    //设置主单字段'是否退货'为明细数据第一条的是否退货标识
                    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                        id: '338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',
                        name: 'isReturn',
                        value: isReturn.toString()
                    });
                    if (isReturn.toString() == '1') {
                        pubsub.publish('96a8f6dc59bf49219cbd89d1fbb4eee2.visible', false)  //不显示新增临时物料
                    }
                    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                        id: '338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',
                        name: 'purchaseOrderDetails',
                        value: newData
                    });
                    console.log('明细赋值',Date())
                setTimeout(() => {
                    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                        id: '338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',
                        name: 'init',
                        value: false
                    });
                }, 3000)
            } else {
                pubsub.publish('@@message.error', res.message);
            }
        })
    })
}

init()

```
在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || const dataSource = {
    type:'api',
    serverName:'mdconsole',
    method:'post',
    url:'/sys/userdraft/get',
    bodyExpression:"callback("+JSON.stringify({
        id:eventPayload.draftId
    })+",'')"
}
resolveDataSource({ dataSource }).then(res=>{
    if(res.success || res.code == '0000'){
        const data = JSON.parse(res.data.billInfo),
        { purchaseOrderDetails } = data,
        formData = Object.assign({},data, {
            id: eventPayload.draftId,
            pageId: eventPayload.pageId,
            init:true,
            purchaseOrderDetails:[]
        });
        console.log('请求草稿箱数据---', formData)
        pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
            id: "338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c",
            data: formData
        });
        if(formData.purchasingOrgCode){
            //公司下拉框
            pubsub.publish('f92f2309ad2d4d4f879968f12856bf30.loadData')
        }
        if(formData.companyCode){
            pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                id:'338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',
                name:'companyCode',
                value: formData.companyCode
            });
            //公司带出的货币
            pubsub.publish('f92f2309ad2d4d4f879968f12856bf30.getStandCurrency',formData.companyCode)
        }
        if(formData.purchaseCategory == '0' && formData.expenseFlag == 1) {  //采购类型为标准，费用化标识为是
            pubsub.publish('0eddd2b601224289b4b7408c310a5949.enabled',false);//是否退货
            pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                colIds: ['4d24f13ac2c4415d8cdcf80c34f4a6ce'],//成本中心
                visible: true
            })
        }else {
            pubsub.publish('0eddd2b601224289b4b7408c310a5949.enabled',true);//是否退货
            pubsub.publish('96a8f6dc59bf49219cbd89d1fbb4eee2.visible',false)//不显示临时物料
            pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                colIds: ['4d24f13ac2c4415d8cdcf80c34f4a6ce'],//成本中心
                visible: false
            })
        }
        if(String(formData.isReturn)=='1') {
            pubsub.publish('23e8c60f0c964b14870b963ddde68d7e.visible',false)  //不显示采购申请
            pubsub.publish('96a8f6dc59bf49219cbd89d1fbb4eee2.visible',false)  //不显示临时物料
        }else {
            pubsub.publish('23e8c60f0c964b14870b963ddde68d7e.visible',true)  //不显示采购申请
            pubsub.publish('338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c.getcontrolpoint')
        }
        // 若所选择的[采购订单类型]设置为标准采购，并且费用化采购标识为“否”，
        // 并且是否退货为“否”并且点收方式为“送货点收”显示字段[源供应标识]，允许编辑,默认值为“否”,其余情况不显示
        if(formData.purchaseCategory == '0' && formData.expenseFlag == 0 && formData.isReturn==0 && formData.receiveType=='R002') {
            pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                colIds: ['74b0921688664c73acaf3fad7bb7489f'],//源供应标识
                visible: true
            })
        }else {
            pubsub.publish(`2c4a7a16a38845118063ae6e6a409672.setColShowAndHide`, {
                colIds: ['74b0921688664c73acaf3fad7bb7489f'],//源供应标识,源供应商编码/名称
                visible: false
            })
        }
        //供应商下拉框 
        pubsub.publish('5b923847f8b74aecbf8d70a28fea83df.loadData',{clearValue:false})
        setTimeout(()=>{
            if(purchaseOrderDetails && purchaseOrderDetails.length>0){
                pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                    id:'338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',  //页面ID
                    name:'purchaseOrderDetails',  //所要修改的字段
                    value: purchaseOrderDetails  //值
                });
            }
            pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
                id:'338f2b2798d2471a82b380499097437c',  //页面ID
                name:'init',  //所要修改的字段
                value: false  //值
            });
        },1500)
    }else{
        pubsub.publish('@@message.error', res.message);
    }
})
```
</s1>"

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || resolveFetch({fetch:{id: "944dfda01b004a56a64897eca6e28b1a",data:"@@formValues"}}).then(function(result){
    

    resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: "93e3b86bded440baa94b44ac385e1a41", data: "state" } }).then(function (state) {
        console.log(eventPayload)
        let { purchasingOrgCode, purchasingOrgName, plantCode, plantName, companyCode, canSeperateNum, purPlanNo, materialCode,orderUnitCode,materialGroupCode,stockLocationCode } = eventPayload
        // pubsub.publish("7fe222d7571747a684b701ce4031f39f.loadData") //采购组织
        pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
            id: "944dfda01b004a56a64897eca6e28b1a",
            data: [
                { name: "purchasingOrgCode", value: purchasingOrgCode },
                { name: "purchasingOrgName", value: purchasingOrgName },
                { name: "plantCode", value: plantCode },
                { name: "plantName", value: plantName },
                { name: "companyCode", value: companyCode },
                { name: "canSeperateNum", value: canSeperateNum },
                { name: "tempCanSeperateNum", value: canSeperateNum },
                { name: "currentData", value: eventPayload },
                { name: "materialCode", value: materialCode },
                { name: "orderUnitCode", value: orderUnitCode },
                { name: "materialGroupCode", value: materialGroupCode },
                { name: "stockLocationCode", value: stockLocationCode },
            ]
        });
        
        pubsub.publish("944dfda01b004a56a64897eca6e28b1a.findDtl", purPlanNo)
        let { dataSource } = state; //表格当前页所有数据
        let currentIndex = _.findIndex(dataSource, { purPlanId: eventPayload.purPlanId }) //当前数据所在下标
        setActiveRow(currentIndex)
        cancelActiveRow(result.currentIndex)
        pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
            id: "944dfda01b004a56a64897eca6e28b1a",
            name:"currentIndex",
            value:currentIndex
        })
        pubsub.publish("555907488730443ea4ed76a2d7bc4d1d.enabled", true) //上一条
        pubsub.publish("012420f686294c7698398ac5f6155dde.enabled", true) //下一条
        if (currentIndex == 0) {
            // pubsub.publish("@@message.info", "$${PEC.tip.theCurrentDataIsTheFirst}") //当前数据已为第一条
            pubsub.publish("555907488730443ea4ed76a2d7bc4d1d.enabled", false) //上一条
        }
        if (currentIndex == dataSource.length - 1) {
            // pubsub.publish("@@message.info", "$${PEC.tip.theCurrentDataIsTheLastOne}") //当前数据已为最后一条
            pubsub.publish("012420f686294c7698398ac5f6155dde.enabled", false) //下一条
        } else { }
    })
});
/**
 * 设置行激活样式
 */
function setActiveRow(index) {
    pubsub.publish('93e3b86bded440baa94b44ac385e1a41.setRowColor', [{
        // 当前行设置active样式
        rowIndex: index, style: {
            // background: 'rgba(64, 158, 255, 0.2)'
            background: '#DBEDFD'
        }
    }])
}

/**
 * 取消行激活样式
 */
function cancelActiveRow(index) {
    pubsub.publish('93e3b86bded440baa94b44ac385e1a41.setRowColor', [{
        // 上一次选择的恢复默认样式
        rowIndex: index, style: {
            backgroud: 'rgb(240, 240, 240)'
        }
    }])
}
```

```
@@form.init || 
const params = eventPayload.$AllParams.state;
const mode = eventPayload.$AllParams.state.mode

if (mode == 'modify') {
    pubsub.publish("a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5.getMainInfo", _.get(eventPayload, "props.locationState.data"))
    pubsub.publish('86201aaaa6ae4e73ad0ca1a0410940f2.enabled', false);
    pubsub.publish('3c63f606c9934f07b997747149fec512.enabled', false);
    pubsub.publish('843b30e3648c4144a3351384d88eb7ac.visible', true);
    pubsub.publish('15e12aa88df9451a9df275e7a26b55c2.visible', false);
    
    pubsub.publish('a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5-title.setLabel', '$${label.edit}$${label.expertInfo}')  
    pubsub.publish('f8f48ef932524711b725ce6252eeec12.visible', true)

} else {
    pubsub.publish('a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5-title.setLabel', '$${button.new}$${label.expertInfo}')
    pubsub.publish('15e12aa88df9451a9df275e7a26b55c2.visible', true);
    pubsub.publish('843b30e3648c4144a3351384d88eb7ac.visible', false);
    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
        id: 'a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5',
        name: 'title',
        value: '$${label.newExpertInformation}'
    }) // 标题
    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
        id: 'a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5',
        name: 'useStatus',
        value: '1'
    }) // 使用状态默认启用 

    pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
        id: 'a5ab7153aca045c4b73616a9d7e33bd5',
        name: 'expertSex',
        value: 'M'
    }) // expertSex  性别默认男
    // ------以下是优化后的版本,等form.change支持批量后 注释回来--------
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || console.log(eventPayload)
let rowsData = _.get(eventPayload, '$AllParams.customs.rowsData');
let initData = {
    rowsData
}
pubsub.publish("@@form.init", {
    id: "da22429a38bd4c82accf0ef8c4b8a6bf",
    data: initData
});

resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: 'f4402ef4b01e417188d2b85f9e448550', data: '' } }).then(function (res) {
    res.state.dataSource = rowsData;
});
pubsub.publish('f4402ef4b01e417188d2b85f9e448550.setData',rowsData)
if (rowsData.length == 1) {
    setTimeout(() => {
        pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
            id: 'da22429a38bd4c82accf0ef8c4b8a6bf',
            name: 'superiorCostItem',
            value: "0000"
        });
        pubsub.publish('@@form.change', {
            id: 'da22429a38bd4c82accf0ef8c4b8a6bf',
            name: 'attributionNo',
            value: "0"
        });
    })

}


```

```
            id: "9c98e32835ae4048bd323a7445cf33f8",
            data: data
        });
    }

        id: "9c98e32835ae4048bd323a7445cf33f8",
        name: "type",
        value: "new"
    });
} else {
    pubsub.publish('9c98e32835ae4048bd323a7445cf33f8-title.setLabel', '$${label.edit}')

    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "9c98e32835ae4048bd323a7445cf33f8",
        name: "noticeId",
        value: eventPayload.$AllParams.state.id
    });
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || // Type you code ...
function getCompanyData() {
    resolveDataSource({
        dataSource: {
            serverName: "qsc",
            type: 'api',
            method: 'POST',
            url: '/signature/certify/list',
            body: JSON.stringify({ "searchKey": "pageNo|pageSize", "page": 1, "pageSize": 1, "params": { "EQ_certifyTypeCode": 1 } }),
        }
    }).then((response) => {
        // 没有认证类型为公司数据时显示公司认证按钮
        if (response.success) {
            if (!response.data || response.data.length == 0) {
                pubsub.publish("f85ca22e059a4b9db70bc256802ebe21.visible", true);
            } else {
                pubsub.publish("f85ca22e059a4b9db70bc256802ebe21.visible", false);
            }
        }
    });
}
let dataSource = {
    serverName: "qsc",
    type: 'api',
    method: 'POST',
    url: '/signature/certify/haspaycompanycode',
};
resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {
    if (response.success) {
        console.log("编码不为空显示【个人认证】")
        // todo
        if (response.data) {
            pubsub.publish("559eba96383f45a6896233da51b94d52.visible", true);
        }
        getCompanyData();
    } else {
        pubsub.publish("559eba96383f45a6896233da51b94d52.visible", false);
        pubsub.publish("f85ca22e059a4b9db70bc256802ebe21.visible", false);
    }
});

```

```
 * todo:  根据指标获取角标数据

function getTabsNums() {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        let filter = {
            unaccept: {
                "IN_delivery.status": ["WAIT", "RECEIVING"],
                "EQ_cancelFlag": 0,
                "EQ_closeFlag": 0,
            },
            receiving: {
                "IN_delivery.status": ["RECEIVING"],
                "EQ_cancelFlag": 0,
                "EQ_closeFlag": 0,
                "GT_arriveQty": 0,
            },

        }
        let dataSource = {
            type: 'api',
            method: 'post',
            serverName: 'qsc',
            url: '/delivery/detail/tab/count',
            bodyExpression: "callback(" + JSON.stringify(filter) + ")"
        };
        resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {
            resolve(response.data)
        });

    })
}

```

```
/**
 * 单独获取列表角标
 * @url 请求路径
 * @params 请求参数
 * @serverName  服务名
 * @return  总数
 */
function getListNums(url, params, serverName = 'qnr', ) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
        let dataSource = {
            type: 'api',
            method: 'post',
            serverName,
            url,
            body: JSON.stringify(params)
        };
        resolveDataSource({ dataSource: dataSource }).then((response) => {
            resolve(response.pager.totalRecords)
        });
    })
}
```

在页面初始化中可以这样调用
```
 || const { currencyConvert, lineAmountCalc,NP } = window.MAIN_COMMON_UTILS
resolveFetch({ fetch: { id: "e529d6b7b5864ffb9612e12c9ef30a9b", data: "@@formValues" } }).then(function (result) {
    let {currencyCode,companyCode,feeBillDtlList} = result;
    var taxAmount = 0, nonTaxAmount = 0, tax = 0;
    if(feeBillDtlList&&feeBillDtlList.length>0){
        feeBillDtlList.forEach(item => {
            taxAmount = NP.plus(taxAmount , Number(item.taxAmount||0));
            nonTaxAmount = NP.plus(nonTaxAmount , Number(item.nonTaxAmount||0));
            tax = NP.plus(tax , Number(item.tax||0));
        })
        taxAmount = currencyConvert(currencyCode, taxAmount, companyCode).convertAmount
        nonTaxAmount = currencyConvert(currencyCode, nonTaxAmount, companyCode).convertAmount
        tax = currencyConvert(currencyCode, tax, companyCode).convertAmount
    }
    pubsub.publish("@@form.change", {
        id: "e529d6b7b5864ffb9612e12c9ef30a9b",
        data: [
            {name: "taxAmount",value: taxAmount}, 
            {name: "nonTaxAmount",value: nonTaxAmount}, 
            {name: "tax",value: tax}
        ]
    });
});
```
</s1>"
